# Text Elements
a)

if ^ is the beginning char of the regular expression, it is matching the beginning.
if ^ is preceded with a [, it is matching a complement. ^1V4DAayC

b) not sure what they are asking for.

with an input just run it on r of ^r or r$.
maybe r$ is supposed to read -1 or eof?
shouldnt ^r be the same as r. ^n0blaoPS
